#### BACK TO SCHOOL - GET SUPER COOL GIFTS

**ID:** 36612602380569 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 23/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/36612602380569-BACK-TO-SCHOOL-GET-SUPER-COOL-GIFTS](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/36612602380569-BACK-TO-SCHOOL-GET-SUPER-COOL-GIFTS)

<p>Joining the storm of going back to school for students across the country, Oreka brings the extremely interesting minigame "Back to School - Receive extremely cool gifts" with gifts up to 500,000 VND, these gifts will be your companions to step into a new explosive school year.</p>
<p>Details about the minigame are as follows:</p>
<p><strong>1. Participants</strong><br>Anyone who wants to try solving puzzles and receive gifts can participate in the minigame.</p>
<p><strong>2. Minigame rules</strong><br>Step 1: Like and share the post in public mode with the Hashtag #Backtoschool #Oreka<br>Step 2: Solve the puzzle which is a secret crossword with 3 hints from Oreka as shown in the image below<br>Step 3: Comment the correct answer and tag 2 more friends.</p>
<p><strong>Note:</strong><br>- Each Facebook account can only participate in answering once.<br>- Minigame participation time: August 22, 2024 - August 29, 2024.</p>
<p><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/36650334599705" alt="B2S-oÃÇ-chuÃõÃÉ (1).jpg"></p>
<p><strong>3. Prizes</strong><br>The prize is up to 500,000 VND including 01 Tote bag and 01 Elmich 480ml thermos bottle for 2 customers:<br>- 01 Tote bag for the fastest customer: answered correctly and completed all the required steps.<br>- 01 Elmich 480ml thermos bottle for the luckiest customer: randomly selected by Oreka.</p>
<p>Let's wait for the mini game results with Oreka on August 30, 2024!</p>
<p>Thank you for participating in the minigame "Back to School - Receive cool gifts", if you have any questions, please contact Oreka so we can answer them!</p>

#### BOOK READING MONTH - TAKE THE CHALLENGE - BRING GIFTS HOME

**ID:** 30689033601305 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 23/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/30689033601305-BOOK-READING-MONTH-TAKE-THE-CHALLENGE-BRING-GIFTS-HOME](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/30689033601305-BOOK-READING-MONTH-TAKE-THE-CHALLENGE-BRING-GIFTS-HOME)

<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify"><a href="https://forms.gle/4e9H77P6JofMJoQT9" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/30738387363481" alt="thang-doc-sach-campaign-facebook cover.jpg"></a></p>
<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify">Official Announcement of the "<strong>Book Reading Month - Take the Challenge - Bring Gifts Home</strong>" Writing Contest Organized by Oreka</p>
<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify"><strong><span class="wysiwyg-font-size-large">1. Purpose and Participants</span><br></strong><strong>1.1. Purpose<br></strong>- To launch the book reading month in response to Vietnam Book Day on April 21st and World Book and Copyright Day on April 23rd.<br>- To foster a reading movement within the community, enhance awareness of the significant importance of reading for knowledge development, skill enhancement, critical thinking, and education.<br>- To encourage book lovers to share their favorite books or profound messages from books they cherish, thereby inspiring others to read.<br>- To provide a space for those seeking a suitable book for themselves.<br><strong>1.2. Participants<em><br></em></strong>All those who love reading and enjoy sharing great books or profound messages are welcome to<br>participate.</p>
<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify"><strong><span class="wysiwyg-font-size-large">2. Contest Rules</span><br></strong><strong>2.1. Topic<em><br></em></strong>Write a short paragraph introducing your favorite book or a message from a book that deeply resonates with you (if it's a message, include the title of the work so readers can find and read it if interested).<br><strong>2.2. Submission Requirements<em><br></em></strong>- Length:<br>¬† + Minimum of 200 words.<br>¬† + Clear and understandable language.<br>- Content:<br>¬†+ Original work; no plagiarism allowed (Organizers may check for plagiarism, and violating submissions will be disqualified).<br>¬† + Content related to books and meaningful messages within books.<br>¬† + Should serve to promote and encourage reading among the audience.<br><strong>2.3. Number of Submissions<br></strong><span style="font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;">- No limit on the number of participants.<br>- Each participant can submit multiple entries, but only the highest-scoring entry will be considered by the organizers.<br></span></p>
<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify"><strong><span class="wysiwyg-font-size-large">3. Submission Period and Method</span><br></strong><strong>3.1. Event Duration<br></strong>The event will run from April 1st, 2024, to April 29th, 2024, as follows:<br>- April 1st - April 4th: Contest announcement.<br>- April 5th - April 15th: Submission period.<br>- April 16th - April 25th: Voting period.<br>- April 29th: Prize announcement.<br><strong>3.2. Submission Method<em><br></em></strong>- Participants should directly submit their entries via the form provided by Oreka.<br><span style="font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;">Submission form link: </span><a href="https://forms.gle/4e9H77P6JofMJoQT9" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span class="wysiwyg-underline" style="color: #1155cc;">Here</span></a><span style="font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif;"><a href="https://forms.gle/4e9H77P6JofMJoQT9" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">¬†</a><br></span>- Submission period: from April 5th, 2024, to April 15th, 2024.<br>- Oreka will compile and post the entries on its Facebook page on April 16th, 2024, to commence the voting phase.</p>
<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify"><strong><span class="wysiwyg-font-size-large">4. Voting Rules, Scoring, and Prizes</span><br></strong><strong>4.1. Voting Rules<em><br></em></strong>- Voting Rules:<br>Step 1: Like/Follow Oreka's fan page.<br>Step 2: Like or react to the post of the participant you support the most.<br>Step 3: Share the post publicly (each account can only share once).<br>- Scoring:<br>+ 1 reaction = 1 point.<br>+ 1 share = 2 points.<br><em>*Note:¬†</em><br>- Voting period: from April 16th, 2024, to April 25th, 2024.<br>- Final results will be announced on April 29th, 2024.<br>- Participants will be disqualified if Oreka detects any irregularities in the voting process, such as manipulation of likes/reactions or shares...<br><strong>4.2. Prize Structure</strong><br>- Prizes will be based on the total points accumulated through public voting, including 3 main prizes:<br>+ 1 first prize.<br>+ 1 second prize.<br>+ 1 third prize.<br>- Additionally, there will be 1 prize chosen by the organizers.<br>- All participants will receive a small gift from Oreka.<br><em>*Note: Prize structure may be subject to change based on the results and quality of entries. Organizers' decision is final.<br></em><strong>4.3. Prize Details<br></strong>- For public voting prizes:<br>+ First Prize: $300 shopping voucher on Oreka and a book of choice from Oreka's provided list.<br>+ Second Prize: $200 shopping voucher on Oreka and a book of choice from Oreka's provided list.<br>+ Third Prize: $100 shopping voucher on Oreka and a book of choice from Oreka's provided list.<br>- For the organizer's choice prize: $100 shopping voucher on Oreka and a book of choice from Oreka's provided list, valid for one month, single-use only.</p>
<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify"><strong>Refer to the book list for your selection:</strong> <a href="https://www.oreka.vn/mua-ban-sach?priceMax=100000" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">gift list link</a></p>

<p class="wysiwyg-text-align-justify"><br>Thank you for participating in the "<strong>Take the Challenge - Bring Gifts Home</strong>" event. If you have any further questions, please feel free to message Oreka for clarification!</p>

<p>Everyone is welcome to join the challenge with Oreka.</p>
<p><strong>2. Rules</strong> <strong>2.1. The Challenge</strong></p>
<p>Players must find recyclable items in the image and comment the corresponding numbers assigned to those items.</p>
<p><strong>2.2. How to Participate</strong></p>
<p>Comment the numbers that correspond to the recyclable items shown in the image.</p>

</ul>
<p><strong>3.2. Prize Structure</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>5 prizes, each worth <strong>100,000 O2 points</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>4. Terms and Conditions</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Each account may participate only once. Fake accounts created just to win minigames will be disqualified.</li>
<li>Edited comments are <strong>NOT</strong> valid.</li>
<li>If Oreka detects any violations of community standards, cheating, or exploitation, rewards will be revoked and the user‚Äôs account may be suspended or permanently banned.</li>
<li>Oreka reserves the right to change the Terms &amp; Conditions or discontinue the event at any time without prior notice.</li>
<li>O2 points will not be refunded if an account is suspended or the points are unused within their validity period.</li>
<li>Prizes are non-transferable and cannot be exchanged for cash.</li>
<li>Oreka is not responsible for any taxes or legal obligations incurred by the prize winners.</li>
<li>Oreka has the right to use all images related to the event for advertising and branding purposes without requiring additional permissions or compensation.</li>
<li>All disputes related to the event will be resolved at the sole discretion of Oreka.</li>
</ul>

#### READING MONTH: FIND GOOD BOOKS - RECEIVE GIFTS IMMEDIATELY

**ID:** 45765366219929 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 28/8/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/45765366219929-READING-MONTH-FIND-GOOD-BOOKS-RECEIVE-GIFTS-IMMEDIATELY](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/45765366219929-READING-MONTH-FIND-GOOD-BOOKS-RECEIVE-GIFTS-IMMEDIATELY)

<p><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/45765514176793" alt="Thang Sach 202504.webp"></p>
<p>Detailed announcement about the challenge ‚ÄúFind a Good Book - Win a Prize Instantly‚Äù organized by Oreka is as follows.</p>
<p><strong>1. Participants<br></strong>Everyone is welcome to join the challenge with Oreka.</p>
<p><strong>2. Rules</strong></p>
<p><strong>2.1. Challenge<br></strong>Participants must find and comment a screenshot of any book with a green theme or tree-related image on the Oreka Website/App and post it under the official contest post.</p>
<p><strong>2.2. How to participate<br></strong>- Step 1: Access the Oreka App/Website, find a book as required, and comment the screenshot under the official event post.<br>- Step 2: Tag 3 friends to join and include a random 3-digit number (e.g., 001, 999, 123,...)<br>- Step 3: Like and share the official event post publicly with hashtags.</p>
<p><strong>2.3. Duration<br></strong>The event will last for 07 days, from April 15, 2025 to April 21, 2025.<br>Winner announcement date: April 22, 2025.</p>
<p><strong>3. Winner selection and prizes</strong></p>
<p><strong>3.1. How to select winners:<br></strong>- Participants who complete all steps and whose lucky number matches or is the closest lower number to the Northern Vietnam lottery result on April 21, 2025 ‚Äî and submitted the earliest ‚Äî will win the Grand Prize.‚Äã<br>- The next closest lower number submitted correctly and earliest will win the Consolation Prize.‚Äã</p>
<p><strong>3.2. Prize structure and rewards<br></strong>- Grand Prize: A shopping voucher worth 2,000,000 VND on Oreka, valid for 1 month.<br>- Consolation Prize: A shopping voucher worth 500,000 VND on Oreka, valid for 1 month.<br>Winners can contact Oreka to convert the voucher into O2 points<strong>.<br></strong></p>
<p><strong>4. Regulations<br></strong>- Each account can only participate once.<br>- Edited comments will be considered invalid.<br>- In the case of multiple participants having the same lucky number, the earliest comment will be prioritized.<br>- If Oreka detects any violations of community standards or fraudulent behavior, the prize will be revoked and the user's account may be suspended or permanently banned according to Oreka's regulations.<br>- Oreka reserves the right to change the Terms &amp; Conditions or cancel the event without notice.<br>- O2 points will not be refunded if the account is suspended due to community standard violations or if the points are not used within the valid period.<br>- Prizes are non-transferable and cannot be exchanged for cash. Oreka is not responsible for any taxes or legal liabilities incurred by participants.<br>- Oreka reserves the right to use all images and related content from the program for advertising or branding purposes without prior consent or compensation.<br>- In case of any disputes, the final decision rests with Oreka.</p>
<p>Thank you for joining the ‚ÄúFind a Good Book - Win a Prize Instantly‚Äù event by Oreka. If you have any questions, feel free to message Oreka or contact our hotline at 0904 433 126 for support!</p>

#### BACK TO SCHOOL - FREE SHIPPING 15K FOR STUDY BOOK ORDERS

**ID:** 36616686715417 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 23/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/36616686715417-BACK-TO-SCHOOL-FREE-SHIPPING-15K-FOR-STUDY-BOOK-ORDERS](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/36616686715417-BACK-TO-SCHOOL-FREE-SHIPPING-15K-FOR-STUDY-BOOK-ORDERS)

<p><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/36616924230425" alt="B2S-2000x547.jpg"></p>
<p>BACK TO SCHOOL - OLD BOOK COVERS - NEW KNOWLEDGE<br>Get a 15K shipping discount voucher</p>
<p>Back to school season is coming, a new school year is about to begin, Oreka gives unlimited 15K Freeship Vouchers when buying study books to help you prepare for an explosive new school year.</p>
<p>For each order of books in the categories: Textbooks, textbooks; Foreign language books; General knowledge books with a value of 150,000 VND or more, you will receive a 15,000 VND discount on shipping fees. The number of vouchers is unlimited, applicable until the end of the program.</p>
<p><strong>1. Program participants:</strong> All sellers on Oreka</p>
<p><strong>2. Program duration:</strong> from 20/08/2024 - 05/09/2024</p>
<p><strong>3. How to participate:</strong><br>- Step 1: Log in to your Oreka account (If you do not have an account, please register)<br>- Step 2: Choose to buy products in the categories that receive incentives or refer to the following list: <a href="https://www.oreka.vn/en/campaigns/back-to-school-oreka" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Applicable list</a><br>- Step 3: If the order value is from 150,000 VND or more, apply the voucher code OREKAB2S</p>
<p><strong>4. Regulations:</strong><br>- Oreka has the right to revoke the voucher at any time in case it detects signs of fraud, profiteering or violating program regulations.<br>- The number of times you receive a discount voucher is unlimited during the program period.<br>- The voucher value is not transferable and cannot be converted into cash. Oreka is not responsible for any taxes or legal liabilities arising from customers.<br>- Oreka has the right to use images related to the program for advertising purposes, brand communication, contest promotion without having to ask for permission or pay any fees.<br>- If there is a problem arising before, during or after the program, which is outside the current regulations, Oreka reserves the right to discuss and make a decision. If necessary, Oreka can adjust and supplement the program regulations to suit the actual situation without prior notice and without the consent of the participants. In case of dispute, the final decision belongs to Oreka.</p>
<p>Choose to buy used books on Oreka to start an exciting new school year!</p>

#### EARTH DAY - SMALL ACTIONS FOR A GREENER EARTH

**ID:** 44994653702937 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 27/3/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44994653702937-EARTH-DAY-SMALL-ACTIONS-FOR-A-GREENER-EARTH](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44994653702937-EARTH-DAY-SMALL-ACTIONS-FOR-A-GREENER-EARTH)

<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;" data-pm-slice="1 1 []"><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/45018674920601" alt="2503-NgaÃÄy-Tƒê-cover-fb.jpg"></p>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;" data-pm-slice="1 1 []">Earn up to 100,000 O2 points when listing products for sale.</p>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;">Can you believe it? Every used item carries a story, a journey, and a unique beauty. An item that seems worthless to one person may be a treasure to another. By preserving and giving them a new life, you are not only allowing their story to continue but also planting seeds of happiness and sustainability for our Earth.</p>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;">To celebrate Earth Day, Oreka is launching the program "<strong>Small Actions for a Greener Earth</strong>." From April 5 to April 20, 2025, for every product listing, we will r<strong>eward you with 500 O2 points</strong> as a token of appreciation for your small but impactful action in making the Earth greener.</p>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;"><strong>1. Eligible Participants: </strong>All Oreka users.</p>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;"><strong>2. Program Duration: </strong>From April 5, 2025 - April 20, 2025.</p>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;"><strong>3. How to Participate:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Step 1: Log in to your Oreka account (If you don‚Äôt have an account, please sign up).</li>
<li>Step 2: List the products you wish to sell.</li>
<li>Step 3: Oreka will review and approve listings that meet the requirements for earning O2 points.</li>
<li>Step 4: The corresponding O2 points for successfully approved listings will be credited to your Oreka account within 24 hours.</li>
</ul>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;"><strong>4. Regulations:</strong></p>
<ul style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;" data-spread="false">
<li>
<p>The program <strong>only applies to manually listed products</strong> and does not apply to automated listings via API.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Each account can receive a maximum of 100,000 O2 points.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>O2 points are valid for one year and cannot be converted into cash.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>O2 points will <strong>not be awarded</strong> if the listing <strong>does not meet the requirements</strong> upon review (e.g., items are completely unusable, the price is unreasonable compared to the product‚Äôs quality, misleading descriptions, spam listings, etc.).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>If Oreka detects that a user violates community standards or engages in fraudulent activities to exploit the program, O2 points will be revoked, and the account may be locked according to Oreka‚Äôs policies.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Oreka is not responsible for any taxes or legal obligations incurred by users.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Oreka reserves the right to modify the terms or discontinue the program at any time without prior notice or liability to any party.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>In case of any disputes related to the program, Oreka's decision will be final.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><a href="https://www.oreka.vn/en/product/upload" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/44994924501913" alt="Frame 427322051.png"></a></p>
<p>¬†</p>
<p style="caret-color: #000000; color: #000000; font-style: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; letter-spacing: normal; orphans: auto; text-align: start; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; widows: auto; word-spacing: 0px; -webkit-text-stroke-width: 0px; text-decoration: none;">If you need assistance during the program, please contact our customer support hotline at 090.4433.126.</p>

<p><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/48409599573785" alt="Thiet Bi Dien 2506.webp" width="1200" height="628"></p><p>Earn up to 100,000 O2 Points &amp; Get 100% Selling Fee Refund!</p><p>That phone was once your everyday companion. That laptop stayed with you through many late-night work sessions. Familiar household appliances like refrigerators, air conditioners, or washing machines‚Ä¶ were by your family's side through all kinds of weather. Even after these ‚Äúold friends‚Äù have fulfilled their duties in your home, remember ‚Äî they still hold value and can continue their journey with other families.</p><p>Sell your used electronics on Oreka! Not only will this help tidy up your living space, but it also extends the product‚Äôs lifecycle and significantly reduces electronic waste ‚Äî a small action that contributes to a greener planet.</p><p>And especially this July, when you successfully list and sell your used electronic devices on Oreka, you can <strong>earn up to 100,000 O2 points</strong> and <strong>get 100% of your selling fees refunded</strong>!</p><p>"What are you waiting for? Old electronics? Sell now ‚Äì enjoy extra rewards!"</p><h3 id="h_01JYZAZ7QH4ZXSSTQTKDZB6CHY"><strong>1. Eligible Participants:</strong></h3><p>All Oreka users.</p><h3 id="h_01JYZAZ7QHKXKTK0TTK88HRT13"><strong>2. Program Period:</strong></h3><p>From July 1, 2025 to July 31, 2025.</p><h3 id="h_01JYZAZ7QH6H8J2K39TVJSJ56M"><strong>3. How to Participate:</strong></h3><ul>
<li>Step 1: Log in to your Oreka account (or sign up if you don't have one yet).</li>
<li>Step 2: List the electronic products you want to sell.</li>
<li>Step 3: Select the ‚ÄúElectronics‚Äù category to receive rewards.</li>
<li>Step 4: Oreka will review and approve your listing.</li>
<li>Step 5: The corresponding O2 points (200 O2 points for each successfully approved listing) will be credited to your Oreka account within 7 days after approval.</li>
<li>Step 6: If the product is sold within 90 days of being listed, the <strong>7.9% service fee</strong> and <strong>2% payment fee</strong> will be refunded to your ‚Äú<strong>My Wallet</strong>‚Äù balance.</li>
</ul><h3 id="h_01JYZAZ7QH0FKGAQY3FYYSKEH8"><strong>4. Terms &amp; Conditions:</strong></h3><ul>
<li>This program <strong>only applies to manually posted listings</strong> and does not apply to listings submitted via API.</li>
<li>Each successfully listed product will earn <strong>200 O2 points</strong>. The maximum number of points per account is <strong>100,000 O2 points</strong>.</li>
<li>O2 points are valid for <strong>1 year</strong> and <strong>cannot be exchanged for cash</strong>.</li>
<li>O2 points <strong>will not be awarded</strong> for listings that fail quality checks: non-functional products, unreasonable pricing, misleading descriptions, spam, etc.</li>
<li>Selling fees will be <strong>refunded to your ‚ÄúMy Wallet‚Äù balance</strong> once Oreka completes the payment for the order.</li>
<li>Fees <strong>will not be refunded</strong> if the account is suspended due to community standards violations or if the order is not completed within 90 days from the listing date.</li>
<li>Oreka is not responsible for any taxes or legal obligations arising from the customer side.</li>
<li>Oreka reserves the right to change the terms or terminate the program without prior notice.</li>
<li>For any disputes arising related to this program, Oreka reserves the final decision.</li>
</ul><p><a href="https://www.oreka.vn/product/upload" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><img src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/48409642566297" alt="Frame 427322051.png" width="3000" height="256"> ¬†</a></p><p>If you need support during the campaign period, please contact our customer service hotline at <strong>090.4433.126</strong>.</p>

#### SEASON SHIFT IS ON ‚Äî SAY FAREWELL TO OLD STUFF!

**ID:** 51149012781209 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 1/10/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/51149012781209-SEASON-SHIFT-IS-ON-SAY-FAREWELL-TO-OLD-STUFF](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/51149012781209-SEASON-SHIFT-IS-ON-SAY-FAREWELL-TO-OLD-STUFF)

<figure class="wysiwyg-image"><img style="aspect-ratio: 1840/700;" src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/51167690883225" alt="2509-Season-change-cover.jpg" width="1840" height="700"></figure><p>GET UP TO 100,000 O2 POINTS AND 100% SALES FEE REFUND WHEN YOU LIST ITEMS IN OCTOBER!</p><p>When the chilly autumn breeze arrives, it‚Äôs time to swap out summer‚Äôs T-shirts and light dresses for warmer outfits. Join Oreka to ‚Äúsay goodbye to old clothes‚Äù ‚Äî refresh your wardrobe, and welcome new trends and fresh energy for a vibrant fall-winter season.</p><p>To celebrate the change of seasons, Oreka offers a special promotion this October: <strong>Get up to 100,000 O2 points and a 100% refund on sales fees</strong> for all clothing items listed<strong> during October.</strong></p><p>Simple, fast, and super cost-saving ‚Äî what are you waiting for? <strong>‚ÄúSeason‚Äôs changing ‚Äì Time to say goodbye to old clothes!‚Äù</strong></p><h3 id="h_01K6D9FTF72W0F4SXJRFZB374M">
<strong>1. Eligible Participants:</strong>¬†</h3><p>All Oreka users.</p><h3 id="h_01K6D9FZJ7NX0ZBGAGHFXE1QSK">
<strong>2. Program Duration:</strong>¬†</h3><p>From <strong>October 1, 2025</strong> to <strong>October 31, 2025</strong>.</p><h3 id="h_01K6D9GRX59FNP3GEESVWWK1H8"><strong>3. How to Participate:</strong></h3><ul>
<li>Step 1: Log in to your Oreka account (sign up if you don‚Äôt have one).</li>
<li>Step 2: List the <strong>pre-owned clothing</strong> items you want to sell.</li>
<li>Step 3: Select categories <strong>‚ÄúWomen‚Äôs Fashion‚Äù and ‚ÄúMen‚Äôs Clothing‚Äù</strong> to qualify for the offer.</li>
<li>Step 4: Oreka will review and approve listings that meet the requirements to earn O2 points.</li>
<li>Step 5: O2 points (200 points per approved listing) will be credited to your Oreka account within 7 days after approval. If the product is <strong>successfully sold within 90 days from the listing date</strong>, all sales fees (7.9% service fee and 2% payment fee) will be <strong>refunded to your balance</strong> in ‚ÄúMy Wallet‚Äù.</li>
</ul><h3 id="h_01K6D9GWMF1BKQYW7TFVVPJ4EV"><strong>4. Terms &amp; Conditions:</strong></h3><ul>
<li>The promotion <strong>only applies to manually listed items</strong>, not for automatic API listings.</li>
<li>Each approved listing earns <strong>200 O2 points</strong>. The maximum reward per account is <strong>100,000 O2 points</strong>.</li>
<li>O2 points are valid for <strong>1 year</strong> and <strong>cannot be converted to cash</strong>.</li>
<li>O2 points <strong>will not be credited</strong> if the listing <strong>does not meet requirements</strong> upon review (e.g., unusable products, unreasonable pricing, misleading descriptions, spam, etc.).</li>
<li>Sales fees will be <strong>refunded to your balance</strong> in ‚Äú<strong>My Wallet</strong>‚Äù when Oreka settles the order payment to you.</li>
<li>Sales fees <strong>will not be refunded</strong> if the account is suspended for community guideline violations or if the order is not completed within 90 days of listing.</li>
<li>Oreka <strong>is not responsible</strong> for any taxes or liabilities arising for users.</li>
<li>In case of disputes, Oreka reserves the final decision.</li>
<li>If Oreka detects violations of community standards or fraudulent activities, the offer will be canceled, and the user‚Äôs account may be suspended, subject to Oreka‚Äôs policies.</li>
<li>Oreka reserves the right to amend the Terms &amp; Conditions or terminate the promotion without prior notice or liability.</li>
</ul><figure class="wysiwyg-image"><a href="https://www.oreka.vn/en/product/upload"><img style="aspect-ratio: 3000/256;" src="https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/article_attachments/51167687842713" alt="EN-Join-now.png" width="3000" height="256"></a></figure><p>For support during the program, please contact our customer care hotline: 090.4433.126.</p>

**ID:** 50195534318489 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2025
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/50195534318489-SMART-HOUSE-CLEANING-GET-THOUSANDS-OF-DISCOUNTS](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/50195534318489-SMART-HOUSE-CLEANING-GET-THOUSANDS-OF-DISCOUNTS)

<p>That‚Äôs why regular decluttering is important ‚Äî and even better when you do it smartly by selling unused household items on Oreka. Not only does it refresh and tidy up your living space, but it also extends the life of old items and helps protect the environment.</p>
<p>Especially this September, when you declutter and sell on Oreka, you‚Äôll unlock big rewards: <strong>Earn up to 100,000 O2 points</strong> for successful listings and enjoy <strong>100% refund of your selling fees</strong>.</p>
<p>So what are you waiting for? Declutter smart ‚Äì collect great rewards today!</p>

<li>Step 6: If the item sells within 90 days of posting, <strong>all selling fees (7.9% service fee + 2% payment fee)</strong> will be refunded to your ‚Äú<strong>My Wallet</strong>‚Äù balance.</li>

## üìÇ Buyer Flow

### üìã Buyer Guidelines 

#### Buyer Guidelines

**ID:** 900006900243 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006900243-Buyer-Guidelines](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006900243-Buyer-Guidelines)

<p>Oreka creates a safe and user-friendly marketplace. If an item is not as described, a Buyer can submit a complaint to Oreka within 3 days. First, discuss with the Seller to give them a chance to fix the problem. If no agreement is reached after 3 days, Oreka will intervene to resolve the issue.</p>
<p>Buyers will only have their complaint processed if they follow the Buyer guidelines:</p>
<p>Do not purchase prohibited items.</p>
<p>Check the product upon delivery and do not rate the Seller unless you are satisfied,<br>You have 3 days from the date of successful delivery to submit a complaint.<br>If you do not contact Oreka within 3 days of receiving the item, an automatic review will be initiated.<br>Once the Buyer has rated the Seller, the transaction is changed to "Completed" status, which means the Buyer can no longer submit a complaint.</p>

---

### üìã Buying items

#### Item Condition

**ID:** 4404877172249 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4404877172249-Item-Condition](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4404877172249-Item-Condition)

<p>For each product listed, the seller will rate and label the product accordingly to describe its condition:</p>
<p>* New: Brand new with tags, unopened box/package, unused.<br>* Like new: Brand new with tags, unopened box/package, unused.<br>* Good: Used, fully functional, working well (may have a few small scratches)<br>* Average: Used, fully functional. Many minor flaws or defects.<br>* Poor: Used. Many flaws. May be damaged (details if damaged).</p>
<p>Please read the product description carefully and check the product photos/videos before buying!</p>

---

#### Payment Methods

**ID:** 4404877194649 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4404877194649-Payment-Methods](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/4404877194649-Payment-Methods)

<p>Buyers can use the following payment methods:</p>
<p>* Visa/Master/JCB credit card</p>
<p>* Debit card</p>
<p>* Bank transfer</p>
<p>* Payment by QR code</p>
<p>* Cash on delivery (COD)</p>
<p>Products on Oreka are used products sold by retailers, so there will be no VAT invoice. Buyers who want to buy in large quantities or need a VAT invoice, please contact Oreka for support.</p>

---

#### Receive Order Notifications

**ID:** 37272057024921 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 4/9/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/37272057024921-Receive-Order-Notifications](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/37272057024921-Receive-Order-Notifications)

<p>Oreka will notify you about the status of your order (Order Confirmed, Order in transit, etc.) through two main methods:</p>
<p>¬†</p>
<p><strong>1. Notifications from the Oreka app</strong></p>
<p>- Use our app to receive instant notifications and make sure you don't miss any orders.</p>
<p>¬†</p>
<p><strong>2. Email Notifications:</strong></p>
<p>- Oreka will update your order status continuously via email. Please check your email regularly to make sure you don't miss any orders.</p>
<p>- Sometimes, emails from Oreka may be placed in your Spam or Promotions folder. Please check these folders to make sure you receive all the necessary information. If you see an email from us in your Spam folder, move it to your Inbox so that future emails from Oreka will always appear in your main folder.</p>
<div id="eJOY__extension_root" class="eJOY__extension_root_class" style="all: unset;">¬†</div>

---

#### Shipping Fee

**ID:** 900005677566 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677566-Shipping-Fee](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677566-Shipping-Fee)

<p>If the product is listed as Free Shipping, the Seller will prepay for shipping the product to you and you will simply pick up the product.</p>
<p>If the product is not eligible for Free Shipping, you will be charged additional shipping costs when you pick up your order.</p>

---

#### The overall transaction

**ID:** 900005677506 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677506-The-overall-transaction](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677506-The-overall-transaction)

<p>1. Explore thousands of products posted on Oreka to choose the item you like. Add that product to the cart and pay for the order in the cart.</p>
<p>2. After receiving your order, within 72 hours, the Seller will confirm the order.</p>
<p>3. After the order has been confirmed, within 03 days (72 hours), the Seller will send the goods to the shipping unit.</p>
<p>4. After receiving the product, if there are no complaints, please help Oreka rate the order by clicking the "Rate" button on the Purchase Order page within 3 days.</p>
<p>*If the Buyer has any complaints about the order, please notify Oreka via the "Complaint" section.</p>

---

### üìã Payment

#### Buyer Protection

**ID:** 900006621043 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621043-Buyer-Protection](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621043-Buyer-Protection)

<p>Oreka commits to fully refund the Buyer if the product is not delivered to you.</p>
<p>In case the product delivered to you is not the same as the product description, Oreka will protect your rights.</p>
<p>First of all, to resolve the problem amicably for both parties, please discuss with the Seller about the problem you have with the product. If both parties do not reach an agreement, after 03 working days, Oreka will intervene to support the resolution.</p>

---

## üìÇ Claim/Cancellation/Returns/Refunds

### üìã Cancellation & Refunds

#### By Buyer

**ID:** 900006621083 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621083-By-Buyer](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621083-By-Buyer)

<p>The cancellation fee will depend on when you request to cancel your order:</p>
<p>a) Before the order is confirmed: no cancellation fee will be charged.</p>
<p>b) After the order has been confirmed: the Buyer must notify the seller via the Chat section on Oreka as soon as possible about the cancellation request.</p>
<p>- If the product has not been dispatched and/or the seller allows cancellation, Oreka will deduct 5% of the order value as a cancellation fee and refund the remaining amount to the Buyer's original payment method.</p>
<p>- If the product has been dispatched and/or the seller does not allow cancellation, the order will not be cancelled and sent to you as scheduled.</p>
<p>*If the Seller allows cancellation with additional fees, this fee will be calculated in addition to the 5% cancellation fee.</p>
<p>c) In the event that the Buyer disputes the order upon receipt and Oreka approves the dispute, the Buyer will receive a refund for the order.</p>
<p><span data-sheets-value='{"1":2,"2":"Depending on the timing of the cancellation, your transaction will be subject to a cancellation fee:\n\na) Before the order is confirmed: no cancellation fee will be charged.\n\nb) After the order is confirmed: at this stage please talk to the seller via Oreka Message as soon as possible about you wanting to cancel the transaction.\n\n- If the item has not been sent out yet and/or the seller allows you to cancel, we will subtract 5%* from your payment as processing fee and refund the remaining amount to your original payment method.\n- If the item has been sent out and/or the seller does not allow you to cancel, the order will be shipped out as planned and no refunds will be available. \n\n*if the seller allows to cancel the order but with extra fee, this extra fee will be charged together with the 5% cancellation fee. \n\nc) In case, the buyer makes a report against the item upon receiving it &amp; Oreka approves of this claim, Oreka will refund full paid amount to the buyer. "}' data-sheets-userformat='{"2":897,"3":{"1":0},"10":1,"11":4,"12":0}'>¬†</span></p>

---

#### By seller

**ID:** 900005677826 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677826-By-seller](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005677826-By-seller)

<p>The cancellation fee will depend on when you request to cancel the order:</p>
<p>a) Before the order is confirmed: when the order notification arrives, the Seller can cancel the order 2 times/month without any fee. From the 3rd cancellation, the cancellation fee will be calculated as 5% of the order value. This is to encourage sellers to regularly update their products, avoiding the case where the Buyer has paid but the goods are not available.</p>
<p>b) After the order is confirmed: from this point, if the Seller wants to cancel the order or not ship the order to the Buyer, the cancellation fee will be calculated as 10% of the order value.</p>

---

#### How long does it take to get a refund?

**ID:** 900006621103 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621103-How-long-does-it-take-to-get-a-refund](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621103-How-long-does-it-take-to-get-a-refund)

<p>The refund process usually takes about 5 days from the time Oreka confirms the refund to the customer. The refund will be returned to the original payment method used by the buyer.</p>

<p>During the transaction, if there is any problem, please discuss on Oreka's Message system.</p>
<p>If both parties cannot reach a common agreement, Oreka will intervene to support the resolution.</p>

### üìã Returns 

#### Returns

**ID:** 900006621923 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 15/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621923-Returns](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006621923-Returns)

<p>After receiving the order, the Buyer has 3 days to submit a product return request. Please DO NOT rate the order.</p>
<p>Discuss the order with the Seller. In case both parties cannot reach a mutual agreement, Oreka will intervene to support the resolution.</p>
<p>The product is eligible for a return request if it meets one of the following conditions:</p>
<p>* The product received is not as described.</p>
<p>* The Seller sent the wrong item or some important components/accessories are missing/missing.</p>
<p>* The product is defective or damaged without the Seller notifying the Buyer in advance.</p>
<p>The product is not refundable if it falls under one of the following cases.</p>
<p>* The product received is as described.</p>
<p>* The product does not fit.</p>
<p>* The Buyer changes his mind about the order.<br>* The Buyer has completed rating the seller.</p>
<p>* The return request is made after 3 days from the time of completion of delivery.<br>* Buyers and Sellers transact business on their own, orders are made outside of Oreka.</p>
<p>¬†</p>

#### Account blocked - reasons & unblocking

**ID:** 900005675546 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 1/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005675546-Account-blocked-reasons-unblocking](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005675546-Account-blocked-reasons-unblocking)

<p>Oreka will block the user's account in the following cases:<br>- Case 1: Violating Oreka's Prohibited Behavior Regulations or contrary to the Law, causing direct or indirect damage/impact on Oreka.<br>- Case 2: Logging in with incorrect account information or password more than 5 times.</p>
<p>In case your account is locked, please contact us via email hotro@oreka.vn or hotline/Zalo 0904433126 with detailed content, Oreka will verify and support the resolution as soon as possible</p>

In such case, you can create a new account with Oreka for free &amp; start over.</span></p>

#### O2 Points

**ID:** 900006618163 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 14/11/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006618163-O2-Points](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006618163-O2-Points)

<p>O2 points are bonus points that Oreka gives to both Sellers and Buyers at Oreka after each successful transaction.</p>
<p>With O2 points, you can accumulate points and use them for future transactions. For every 1,000 VND spent through a transaction (selling or buying), you will accumulate 1 O2 point.</p>
<p>1 O2 point equals to 1 VND. For example, when purchasing at OREKA, if you have 1,000 O2 points, you can use that to get 1,000 VND discount from the payment amount.</p>
<p>O2 points are valid for one year. For example, if you are awarded points on November 15, 2020, these points will expire on November 14, 2021.</p>
<p>Older O2 points will be used first.</p>
<p>*Note: O2 points cannot be used to replace/convert to cash or withdraw money.</p>

#### Communication Policy

**ID:** 900005933826 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005933826-Communication-Policy](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900005933826-Communication-Policy)

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">This policy describes how Oreka communicates with you electronically. We may amend this policy at any time by posting a revised version on our website. The revised version will be effective at the time we post it.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">You agree and consent to receive all communications, agreements, documents, and notices electronically (collectively, ‚ÄúCommunications‚Äù) that we provide in connection with your Oreka account (‚ÄúAccount‚Äù) and your use of our Services. Communications include:</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Agreements and policies to which you agree (e.g., the Oreka Terms of Service and the Oreka Privacy Policy), including updates to such agreements or policies;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Transaction receipts or confirmations;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Account statements and history;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Authority statements that we are required to provide to you; and any other Account, Oreka Fund account, or transaction information.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">We will provide these Notices to you by posting them on the Oreka website and/or by sending them via email to you at the primary email address listed in your Oreka profile.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Update Your Contact Information</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">It is your responsibility to keep your primary email address up to date so that Oreka can communicate with you electronically. You understand and agree that if Oreka sends you an electronic Communication that you do not receive because your primary email address on file is inaccurate, out of date, blocked by your service provider, or you are otherwise unable to receive electronic Notices, Oreka will be deemed to have provided the Communication to you.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Please note that if you use a spam filter to block or reroute email from senders not listed in your email address book, you must add Oreka to your email address book in order to receive the Notices we send you. You may update your email address or primary street address at any time by logging into the Oreka app. If your email address is invalid and electronic Notifications sent to you by Oreka are returned, Oreka may consider your Account inactive and you will not be able to transact or have any activity using your Oreka Account until we receive a valid, active primary email address from you.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Hardware and Software Requirements</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">To access and retain Electronic Communications, you will need the following computer hardware and software:</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">A computer or mobile device with Internet access;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">A current web browser that includes 128-bit encryption (e.g., Internet Explorer version 6.0 or later, Firefox version 2.0 or later, Chrome version 3.0 or later, or Safari 3.0 or later) with cookies enabled;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Adobe Acrobat Reader version 8.0 or later to open documents in .pdf format;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">A valid email address (your email address on file with Oreka); sufficient storage space to save previous emails or a printer installed to print them.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">We will notify you if there are any material changes to the hardware or software required to receive Electronic Communications from Oreka. By agreeing, you confirm that you have access to the necessary equipment and can receive, open and print or download a copy of any Notice for your records. You may print or save a copy of this Notice for your records as they may be subject to change at a later date.</span></p>

#### Conflict Resolution Policy

**ID:** 900006681366 | **Votes:** 0 | **Updated:** 31/8/2024
**URL:** [https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006681366-Conflict-Resolution-Policy](https://oreka.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/900006681366-Conflict-Resolution-Policy)

<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Oreka.vn and the Seller are responsible for receiving and handling complaints from Buyers related to transactions on the Oreka.vn Website and other Oreka platforms.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Buyers have the right to send complaints about product quality, services not matching the description, payment information being disclosed causing damage to them to the Management Board of Oreka.vn. After receiving these reflections, we will verify the information, if it is true as reflected, we will propose a solution for both parties including the Buyer and the Seller.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Customers send complaints to the following address:</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">- Oreka Vietnam Co., Ltd.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">- Address: B2-25 Vinhomes Gardenia, Ham Nghi Street, Cau Dien, Nam Tu Liem, Hanoi</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">- Email: hotro@oreka.vn - Phone: 0904433126</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Steps to resolve disputes and complaints</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Step 1: The Company's Customer Care Department will receive complaints from Customers. These Departments will proactively resolve them quickly and immediately respond to the results of resolving complaints based on the Policies announced by the Company.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Step 2: In cases that are complicated or not specified in the policies announced by the Company, the Customer Care Department will commit to a response time for Customers.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">The time to process customer complaints is 24 - 72 hours</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Step 3: Transfer the complaint resolution results to relevant departments for implementation and call to confirm with the Customer that the complaint has been resolved.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Oreka.vn respects and strictly implements the provisions of the law on protecting the rights of Customers. Therefore, Sellers on the Oreka.vn Website are requested to provide complete, accurate, honest and detailed information related to products and services. All acts of fraud and cheating in business are condemned and must bear full responsibility before the law.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">We publicly disclose the mechanism for resolving disputes arising during transactions on the Oreka.vn Website. When a customer purchases goods or services and has a conflict with the Seller or has their legitimate interests damaged, Oreka.vn will provide the Customer with the Seller's registration information immediately after receiving the Customer's request.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">Oreka.vn publicly discloses the dispute resolution mechanism and process for the parties involved: dispute resolution according to the unified agreement exchange mechanism, the parties involved will follow the indirect exchange process via phone, confirmation by email, if still unable to reach an agreement, it will be resolved through a direct meeting to specify the problem, thoroughly resolve the conflict between the parties for the best benefit.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">The parties including the Seller, the Customer and Oreka.vn will have to play a responsible role in actively resolving the problem. For the Seller, it is necessary to be responsible for providing documents certifying information related to the incident that is causing the conflict to the customer. Oreka.vn will be responsible for the arbitration to listen and receive information from the customer (in specific cases, we will: require the customer to be responsible for providing accurate invisible and tangible information about the arising conflict that needs to be resolved and that the customer has seen himself damaged) and the Seller, then proceed to review and clarify, analyze which party is at fault. Get opinions on the agreement on the level of compensation between the two parties and end the dispute in the most satisfactory way.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">In case it is proven that the fault belongs to the Seller, Oreka.vn will take measures to warn, request a refund of all costs that the Customer has had to spend to own that product/service or must exchange the product, service with the quality that the Seller announced on Oreka.vn. If the Seller re-offends, Oreka.vn will terminate and remove all information of that Seller on Oreka.vn.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">¬†</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-weight: normal;">If through negotiation the conflict arising from the transaction cannot be resolved, Oreka.vn will request one of the two parties to seek the intervention of a competent legal authority to ensure the legitimate interests of the parties, especially for the customer.</span></p>
